# Yet Another Mech Variants List

The following list contains a total of 1,579 'mech variants from Mechwarrior 5 with Yet Another Mechlab using the following additional mods:
* Astryn Collection (by Andrew Pappas)
* BM_Arthur (by Arthur Battlemech)
* BM_Dragonslayer (by Koi)
* BM_FireMoth (by KodiakJ)
* BM_Turkina (by KodiakJ)
* Classic Mech Collection Lore YAML (by SankaraSamsara)
* Lore-based Mech Variants - YAML-Edition (by Mace24de)
* OmniCore - Lore-Friendly (by Snafulator)
* Pirate_FrankenMechs v1.1 (by [Volfegan](https://github.com/volfegan/Pirate_FrankenMechs_MW5mod))
* Rifleman III (by phfor)
* Wasp YAML-Edition (by Mace24de / Zombeh)
* Wyvern YAML-Edition (by Mace24de / Zombeh)
* Yet Another IS Mech (by [DeadRaiser](https://www.nexusmods.com/users/41300230))
* Yet Another Legendary Mech (by Malum Umbra)
* Yet Another Mechlab (by [cszolee79 and trueg](https://www.nexusmods.com/mechwarrior5mercenaries/mods/459))
* Yet Another Mechlab Mechs (by [Yet Another Team](https://www.nexusmods.com/mechwarrior5mercenaries/mods/816))
* Yet Another Special Variant (by trueg)
* YetAnotherClanMech (by cszolee79 and trueg)
## Light Mechs
